<dt class="class"><h2><a name="QXmlFormatter" href="#QXmlFormatter">class <span class="class-name">QXmlFormatter</span></a>(PythonQt.PythonQtInstanceWrapper)</h2></dt><dd class="class"><dd>

</dd>  <div class="mro"><dl class="mro"><dt>Method resolution order:</dt><dd><a href="./PythonQt.QtXmlPatterns.html#QXmlFormatter">QXmlFormatter</a></dd><dd>PythonQt.PythonQtInstanceWrapper</dd><dd><a href="./__builtin__.html#object">__builtin__.object</a></dd></dl></div><h4 class="head-methods">Methods </h4><dl class="function"><dt><a name="QXmlFormatter-__init__" href="#QXmlFormatter-__init__"><span class="function-name">__init__</span></a><span class="argspec">(...)</span></dt><dd>

<a name="PythonQt.QtXmlPatterns.QAbstractMessageHandler"></a>

## `QAbstractMessageHandler`
